                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Friday, February 14, 2014
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <a name="8459059538870129376">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     Pedro Matos' Fixie from Portugal
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8459059538870129376" itemprop="articleBody">
                     Hi all, today we want to show you some photos from
                     <b>
                      Pedro Matos
                     </b>
                     , a Portuguese guy in love with his fixie, he created it piece by piece, day by day...great!
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                      <tbody>
                       <tr>
                        <td style="text-align: center;">
                         <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HM_X0Xu2T7g/Uv4i5hASc7I/AAAAAAAAGhw/faPN_cqiX6s/s1600/IMG_20140213_180749.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                          <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HM_X0Xu2T7g/Uv4i5hASc7I/AAAAAAAAGhw/faPN_cqiX6s/s1600/IMG_20140213_180749.jpg" width="640"/>
                         </a>
                        </td>
                       </tr>
                       <tr>
                        <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                         Pedro Matos' Fixie from Portugal
                        </td>
                       </tr>
                      </tbody>
                     </table>
                     Here we have some
                     <b>
                      specifications
                     </b>
                     about this fixie:
                     <br/>
                     <ul>
                      <li>
                       Frame and fork: no brand
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Headset: ahead metro bikes
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Crankset: 44t 170mm
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Cranks/chainring: sram/kingstar
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Bottom bracket: sram 108mm powerspline
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Wheels: no logo; 18t fixed cog
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Tires: kenda 700/28c
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Handlebar: cinelli pepper
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Stem: cinelli ant
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Saddle: selle italia xo
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Chain: kmc
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Grips: cult x vans waffle grips
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Seat post: metro-bikes
                      </li>
                     </ul>
                     <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                      <tbody>
                       <tr>
                        <td style="text-align: center;">

                          <img border="0" height="480" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-IYPuJNNbXNE/Uv4i4r7mgbI/AAAAAAAAGhs/6ScJ6Jzm-34/s1600/DSC_0198.jpg" width="640"/>
                         </a>
                        </td>
                       </tr>
                       <tr>

                 <script type="text/javascript">
                  document.doAT = function(cl)
{
        var myclass = new RegExp('hentry');
        var myTitleContainer = new RegExp('post-title');
        var myPostContent = new RegExp('post-footer');
        var elem = this.getElementsByTagName('div');
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; elem.length; i++)
        {
            var classes = elem[i].className;
            if (myclass.test(classes))
            {                var container = elem[i];
                for (var b = 0; b &lt; container.childNodes.length; b++)
                {
                    var item = container.childNodes[b].className;
                    if (myTitleContainer.test(item))
                    {
                        var link = container.childNodes[b].getElementsByTagName('a');
                        if (typeof(link[0]) != 'undefined')
                        {
                            var url = link[0].href;
                            var title = link[0].innerHTML;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            var url = document.url;
                            var title =  container.childNodes[b].innerHTML;
                        }
                        if (typeof(url) == 'undefined'|| url == 'undefined' ){
                            url = window.location.href;
                        }
                    var singleq = new RegExp("'", 'g');
                    var doubleq = new RegExp('"', 'g');                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                    title = title.replace(singleq, '&#39;', 'gi');
                    title = title.replace(doubleq, '&#34;', 'gi');

                    }
                    if (myPostContent.test(item))
                    {
                        var footer = container.childNodes[b];
                    }
                }
                var n = document.createElement('div');
                var at = "&lt;div class='addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style ' addthis:title='"+title+"' addthis:url='"+encodeURI(url)+"'   &gt; &lt;a class='addthis_button_facebook_like' fb:like:layout='button_count'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a class='addthis_button_tweet'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a class='addthis_button_pinterest_pinit'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a class='addthis_button_google_plusone' g:plusone:size='medium'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a class='addthis_counter addthis_pill_style'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/div&gt; ";
                n.innerHTML = at;
                container.insertBefore(n , footer);
            }
        }
    return true;
};

document.doAT('hentry');
